# Rayon pour les étudiants | 🇫🇷 French | Rayon Docs 

Rayon est **gratuit pour les étudiants et les professeurs !** [**Vous pouvez créer votre compte en cliquant sur ce lien.**](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)

Vous trouverez sur cette page tout ce qui concerne le plan étudiant.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#creation-de-compte)

Création de compte

Pour obtenir un compte étudiant, veuillez suivre les étapes suivantes :

*   Créez un compte Rayon, [sur ce lien](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    , en utilisant l'adresse électronique d'un établissement d'enseignement. Notez que les courriels génériques (comme gmail, hotmail, etc.) ne pourront pas bénéficier d'un compte étudiant. Vous devez avoir une adresse courriel officielle d'un établissement académique reconnu.
    
*   Au cours de l'onboarding, n'oubliez pas de sélectionner l'option "Je suis étudiant".
    
    *   **Si votre école fait déjà partie de notre programme étudiant**, vous serez automatiquement inscrit au plan étudiant.
        
    *   **Si votre école ne fait pas encore partie de notre programme étudiant**, et que vous avez déclaré dans l'onboarding que vous étiez étudiant, vous recevrez un formulaire par email, quelques minutes après votre inscription, vous permettant de soumettre votre candidature pour obtenir un plan étudiant. Si votre candidature est validée, nous vous intégrerons à notre plan étudiant et ajouterons votre université à notre liste d'universités partenaires. De cette manière, tous les étudiants qui s'inscriront à Rayon après vous recevront automatiquement un statut d'étudiant.
        
    
*   **Votre plan étudiant vous donnera accès à toutes les fonctionnalités de notre plan Pro** : exportations sans filigrane, accès à l'ensemble des bibliothèques de Rayon, etc.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#faq)

FAQ

Les questions que les élèves posent habituellement, les réponses que nous donnons habituellement !

**Mon université ne fournit pas de courrier électronique institutionnel aux étudiants. Puis-je vous envoyer ma carte d'étudiant comme preuve ?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#mon-universite-ne-fournit-pas-de-courrier-electronique-institutionnel-aux-etudiants.-puis-je-vous-en)

Malheureusement, non. Les courriels non institutionnels (comme Gmail, Hotmail, etc.) ne pourront pas bénéficier d'un compte étudiant. Nous sommes désolés, mais nous ne sommes pas en capacité de gérer les fraudes liées aux fausses cartes d'étudiant.

**J'ai créé un compte Rayon, mais je n'ai pas mentionné que j'étais étudiant lors de l'inscription. Comment puis-je résoudre ce problème ?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#jai-cree-un-compte-rayon-mais-je-nai-pas-mentionne-que-jetais-etudiant-lors-de-linscription.-comment)

Vous devez supprimer votre compte dans le menu principal > paramètres > supprimer le compte et en créer un nouveau. Pensez bien à utiliser votre adresse mail étudiante lors de la création du compte !

Mon école m'a donné une adresse électronique d'ancien élève ; puis-je l'utiliser pour obtenir un plan étudiant ?[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#mon-ecole-ma-donne-une-adresse-electronique-dancien-eleve-puis-je-lutiliser-pour-obtenir-un-plan-etu)

Malheureusement, non. Nous n'accordons un plan étudiant qu'aux étudiants actifs/inscrits. Les courriels d'anciens élèves ne sont donc pas acceptés.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students#were-always-available)

Nous sommes toujours disponibles !

N'hésitez pas à nous envoyer un courriel à [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#43303633332c31370331223a2c2d6d302c)
.

[PreviousPasser à Rayon](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/switching-to-rayon)
[NextPolitique de remboursement](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy)

# Concevoir un plan de zonage dans Rayon | 🇫🇷 French | Rayon Docs 

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#quest-ce-quun-plan-de-zonage)

Qu'est-ce qu'un plan de zonage ?

Un plan de zonage est un dessin qui définit l’**utilisation autorisée, l’implantation et la taille d’un projet** conformément aux réglementations locales d’urbanisme. Il montre généralement les limites de propriété, les zones constructibles autorisées et les affectations du sol prévues.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631891706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FMSx5wRjNDLpffRWhPfhm%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5598a15308ae9df0ea2d4e93119fb483ee6293bd%252FPreviewer%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d523f1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#comment-creer-un-plan-de-zonage-dans-rayon)

Comment créer un plan de zonage dans Rayon ?

Créer un plan de zonage dans Rayon prend généralement entre 1 et 2 heures, selon la taille et la complexité de la propriété. Pour commencer, vous aurez simplement besoin d’un **fichier DWG ou PDF de la propriété**, ainsi que d’informations sur les règles et réglementations locales applicables à votre projet.

🔗 Voici un lien vers le [modèle de zonage de Rayon](https://www.rayon.design/app/model/f510f416-1e4d-485e-9f76-8c9506b2fd46?canvas=V3VmgEPTVp2&scale=1189.1244713620945&x=184933803.93246838&y=21285201.191463083&token=rayon-template)
. C’est parti !

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#id-1-importer-votre-dessin-5-minutes)

(1) Importer votre dessin : _5 minutes_

L’importation de fichiers dans Rayon est simple.

*   Sélectionnez l’option `Importer DWG/PDF` depuis le menu principal de votre modèle.
    
*   Rayon vous demandera d’évaluer l’échelle de votre dessin.
    

En savoir plus sur l’import [ici](https://docs.rayon.design/french/documentation/models-and-team-management/importing-files)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#id-2-dessiner-une-legende-5-minutes)

**(2) Dessiner une légende :** _**5 minutes**_

Dessinez une légende listant les usages autorisés et l’implantation des bâtiments, puis formatez-la selon les normes locales de dessin.

*   Utilisez l’outil `Rectangle`, puis sélectionnez-le et définissez son `Style` via le panneau latéral droit. Vous pouvez y définir une couleur, un motif de hachures, un type de ligne, etc. Ensuite, **enregistrez et nommez votre style** pour le réutiliser par la suite.
    
*   Utilisez l’outil `Texte` pour ajouter des descriptions à votre légende.
    

En savoir plus sur les styles [ici](https://docs.rayon.design/french/documentation/design/styles)
.

**(3) Dessiner des zones :** _**15 à 30 minutes**_

L’outil `Zone` de Rayon propose deux manières de définir des zones :

*   **Zone en polyligne :** utilisez l’outil `Zone` pour dessiner une forme fermée. L’étiquette affichera **la surface en mètres carrés**, mise à jour automatiquement à chaque modification de la forme.
    
*   **Zone dans un réseau de murs :** commencez par dessiner des `murs` pour définir une zone fermée sur votre plan. Ensuite, utilisez l’outil `Zone` pour remplir cet espace **en un simple clic**. Une étiquette indiquera automatiquement la surface en m² et s’ajustera selon les modifications.
    

En savoir plus sur l’outil zone [ici](https://docs.rayon.design/french/documentation/design/elements-walls-zones-openings-etc)
.

**(4) Créer un tableau de zonage :** _**15 à 20 minutes**_

Listons, comptons et additionnons rapidement vos zones avec l’outil tableau de Rayon !

*   **Nommez vos zones** en les sélectionnant et en modifiant leur propriété `Nom`.
    
*   Ajoutez des **propriétés personnalisées** à vos zones pour faciliter la planification. Par exemple, vous pouvez ajouter une propriété `Catégorie` pour regrouper les usages du sol (Public, Commercial, Résidentiel, etc.).
    

*   **Créez un tableau** listant les zones selon leur catégorie :
    
    *   Créez un nouveau tableau avec le bouton `+`
        
    *   Activez uniquement la catégorie `zone`
        
    *   Ajoutez les propriétés `Aire` et `Catégorie`
        
    *   Groupez le tableau selon la `Catégorie`
        
    *   Vous avez désormais un tableau récapitulatif listant chaque zone avec son nom, sa catégorie, sa surface en m², et les totaux. `Exportez-le` au format Excel !
        
    

En savoir plus sur les tableaux [ici](https://docs.rayon.design/french/documentation/design/metadata-and-tables)
.

**(5) Partagez votre travail :** _**5 minutes**_

Vous êtes à la dernière étape ! Maintenant que vous avez votre plan de zonage architectural et un tableau de données, organisez-les sous forme de `pages` et partagez-les directement depuis Rayon **via un lien URL**.

*   `Importez` votre tableau au format PDF et placez-le à côté de votre plan architectural.
    
*   Ajoutez une `page` sur votre canevas et définissez son **échelle et son format de papier**.
    
*   Ajoutez un **cartouche** depuis la `bibliothèque de blocs` de Rayon et personnalisez-le.
    
*   **Partagez votre travail** via un lien URL en cliquant sur le bouton `Partager`, puis copiez l’URL. Envoyez-le ensuite aux parties prenantes.
    

En savoir plus sur les pages [ici](https://docs.rayon.design/french/documentation/design/pages)
.

Et voilà ! Vous avez terminé les cinq étapes pour créer un plan de zonage dans Rayon. N’hésitez pas à personnaliser et à utiliser le [modèle de zonage de Rayon](https://www.rayon.design/app/model/f510f416-1e4d-485e-9f76-8c9506b2fd46?canvas=V3VmgEPTVp2&scale=1189.1244713620945&x=184933803.93246838&y=21285201.191463083&token=rayon-template)
 pour vos propres projets. 🔗

Pour plus d’instructions détaillées étape par étape, regardez notre tutoriel complet sur la création d’un plan de zonage dans Rayon :

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#nous-sommes-toujours-disponibles)

Nous sommes toujours disponibles !

N’hésitez pas à nous écrire à [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e0939590908f9294a09281998f8ece938f)
.

[PreviousFAQ](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/faq)
[NextDivers](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Qu'est-ce qu'un plan de zonage ?](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#quest-ce-quun-plan-de-zonage)
    
*   [Comment créer un plan de zonage dans Rayon ?](https://docs.rayon.design/french/autres-ressources/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#comment-creer-un-plan-de-zonage-dans-rayon)

# Politique de remboursement | 🇫🇷 French | Rayon Docs 

Chez Rayon, nous nous efforçons de fournir un logiciel de conception fiable et de haute qualité. Nous comprenons que parfois, des situations spécifiques peuvent nécessiter un remboursement ou un ajustement de l'abonnement. **Ce document décrit les conditions dans lesquelles les remboursements sont accordés**, et les cas dans lesquels ils ne sont pas applicables.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#motifs-valables-de-remboursement)

Motifs valables de remboursement

Nous comprenons que de véritables erreurs ou des problèmes techniques peuvent survenir. Des remboursements peuvent être accordés dans les circonstances spécifiques suivantes :

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#id-1.-probleme-technique-majeur-bogue-reproductible)

1\. Problème technique majeur (bogue reproductible)

Si vous rencontrez un dysfonctionnement technique important qui empêche l'utilisation normale du logiciel :

*   Le problème est reproductible et confirmé par notre équipe technique.
    
*   Notre équipe d'assistance a été informée et le problème persiste malgré la résolution des problèmes.
    

Dans ce cas, nous évaluerons la situation et, le cas échéant, nous proposerons un remboursement.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#id-2.-paiement-par-erreur-de-labonnement-annuel)

2\. Paiement par erreur de l'abonnement annuel

Si vous aviez l'intention d'acheter un abonnement mensuel, mais que vous avez accidentellement effectué le paiement pour un abonnement annuel, nous pouvons vous aider :

*   Vous informez notre équipe d'assistance dans les 4 semaines suivant la date d'achat.
    
*   Vous n'avez pas utilisé le logiciel de manière intensive pendant cette période (évaluée à notre discrétion).
    

Dans ce cas, nous pouvons convertir votre abonnement annuel en abonnement mensuel et vous rembourser la différence.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#id-3.-eligibilite-aux-reductions-pour-les-etudiants)

3\. Éligibilité aux réductions pour les étudiants

Rayon offre un accès gratuit aux étudiants inscrits. Si vous :

*   avez acheté un plan payant tout en étant éligible pour une licence étudiante gratuite.
    
*   nous fournissez une preuve valide d'inscription active, telle qu'une adresse électronique institutionnelle.
    

Nous rembourserons le paiement du mois en cours après vérification. Veuillez noter que les remboursements ne s'appliquent pas rétroactivement au-delà du cycle de facturation en cours.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#id-4.-double-paiement)

4\. Double paiement

Vous avez rencontré la situation exceptionnelle où notre système vous a facturé deux fois ; bien que ce soit très rare, cela peut arriver, et nous vous rembourserons bien sûr, si vous pouvez nous envoyer la preuve des paiements.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#motifs-de-remboursement-non-eligibles)

Motifs de remboursement non éligibles

Dans un souci d'équité et de clarté opérationnelle, les situations suivantes ne sont pas considérées comme des motifs valables de remboursement ou d'annulation de l'abonnement :

*   Manque d'utilisation : Le fait de ne pas utiliser votre compte Rayon ne donne pas droit à un remboursement. Les abonnements sont renouvelés automatiquement, sauf en cas d'annulation, quelle que soit la fréquence d'utilisation.
    
*   Renouvellement automatique : Les abonnements se renouvellent automatiquement à moins d'être annulés ; le fait de ne pas respecter la date limite d'annulation ou d'oublier d'annuler n'est pas considéré comme une raison valable.
    
*   Insatisfaction basée sur les préférences : Le fait de décider que vous n'aimez tout simplement pas le logiciel ou de constater qu'il ne correspond pas à vos préférences personnelles après l'achat ne constitue pas un motif de remboursement.
    
*   Modification des besoins ou de l'état d'avancement du projet : si vos projets changent, sont annulés ou si vous n'avez plus besoin de Rayon, ces raisons ne sont pas considérées comme valables pour un remboursement.
    
*   Attentes de tiers : Aucun remboursement ne sera effectué sur la base de comparaisons avec d'autres logiciels ou d'attentes non satisfaites sur la base d'évaluations externes.
    

Nous encourageons vivement tous les utilisateurs à explorer notre offre et nos fonctionnalités avant de s'engager dans un plan payant afin de s'assurer que Rayon répond à leurs besoins.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#comment-demander-un-remboursement)

Comment demander un remboursement

Pour demander un remboursement dans le cadre des scénarios éligibles décrits ci-dessus :

1.  Contactez notre équipe d'assistance à [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3a494f4a4a55484e7a485b435554145e5f49535d54)
     ou contactez-nous via le chat d'assistance de l'application.
    
2.  Fournissez des détails pertinents tels que :
    

*   Votre adresse électronique enregistrée.
    
*   La description du problème ou de la raison du remboursement.
    
*   Toute preuve requise (par exemple, l'adresse électronique de l'établissement pour la vérification de l'étudiant).
    

1.  Notre équipe examinera votre demande et vous répondra dans les 5 jours ouvrables.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/refund-policy#notes-finales)

Notes finales

*   Les remboursements sont effectués selon le mode de paiement initial.
    
*   Nous nous réservons le droit de refuser les demandes de remboursement qui ne répondent pas aux conditions énoncées ci-dessus.
    
*   Nous encourageons tous les utilisateurs à consulter nos tarifs et nos ressources d'assistance avant de s'engager dans un plan payant. [Plus d'informations ici](https://rayon.design/pricing)
    .
    

Pour toute question, veuillez contacter notre équipe d'assistance à l'adresse [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 - nous sommes là pour vous aider !

[PreviousRayon pour les étudiants](https://docs.rayon.design/french/others/rayon-for-students)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Start here! | Rayon Docs 

**Welcome to Rayon!** Let's get started, simply **follow the steps below**...

1

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/start-here#what-is-rayon)

What is Rayon?

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/start-here#rayon-is-the-effortless-cad-software-for-drawing-perfect-architectural-drawings)

**Rayon is the** _**effortless**_ **CAD software for drawing perfect architectural drawings.**

**It is a one stop-shop to import, draft, stylize and layout** your work, so as to produce professional-grade document sets. Rayon represents the next generation of tools for architects: online, collaborative, cross-OS, ergonomic. Rayon offers a newer, fresher approach to CAD, one that many have been expecting for a long time.

2

###

**A video is worth a thousand words**: here is a 20-minute demo, where we will walk you through a short presentation of our software.

# Your workspaces | Rayon Docs 

Once your account is created, you will reach the project manager, where files are stored. The project manager is organized into workspaces. This page will take you step-by-step through **your first steps in the project manager.**

1

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/your-workspaces#your-personal-workspace)

Your personal workspace

Your `**Personal**` workspace should now look like this...

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FTRyJVa7ujSZmR3VFxBYO%252FFrame%25201767%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D647e735f-add8-41aa-8a9b-4d390ae68ba6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=323b1bc0&sv=2)

A few important things...

*   At the centre of the screen are **your models.**
    
*   The bar on the left displays **all your workspaces** (repositories for your models...more on that later).
    
*   In the top left corner is **your avatar**, where you have access to your profile and its settings.
    
*   On the right side of the screen are the `**New**` and `**Import**` buttons, as well as some information about the **current workspace and billing**.
    

2

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/your-workspaces#h_2de1be442b)

Starting a new project

You can start a new project from your `**Personal**` workspace in 2 different ways:

*   `**+ New model**` allows you to create a new drawing.
    
*   `**Import**` allows you to import a file (JPG\\PNG image, DWG, DXF & PDF).
    

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FCzOKp4czYHolFUjD3a96%252Fnew-proejct-1-ezgif.com-optimize.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32ab587c-86eb-483d-ba09-cd4710c8bd53&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb5745be&sv=2)

3

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/your-workspaces#next-step)

Next step

You are done! Head to the next step, **click below!**

[Next step](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/creating-a-new-project)

. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)

# Signing up | Rayon Docs 

Let's start by **creating a free Rayon account**. It will take you less than a minute...

1

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#head-to-the-signup-page)

Head to the signup page

To create a new account, [Signup here](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/signup)

2

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#h_75510a44f2)

Enter your information

...and click on `**Create account**`**.**

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Fl4UGZX0HRGH3NSKutpdG%252FFrame%25201757%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D821e0e56-f835-4a6b-a7f2-76a77d21bc2d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d18e956d&sv=2)

3

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#h_df1f293b51)

Just a few questions...

The next few steps will be about getting to know you!

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FHUgTNd0ZjMwN2Onv3e4i%252FFrame%25201759%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbd73a93-d4b6-4252-9bd1-30cdf8b97d19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c178f24&sv=2)

4

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#h_9b5c24fd05)

Alone or in team?

You can now either continue or your own, or create a team! If you choose to start a team, you will be asked to **choose a name for your organization**, and to fill in the few survey questions.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FpYJwkc16a1rcLGHx87ly%252FFrame%25201761.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51fc5c26-6306-432c-bab7-1dceb5f4600e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7b60744&sv=2)

Then, **invite colleagues** to your organization. Each member can be invited as:

*   **Admin**: a member that will be able to **see and edit all files and settings** of your organization.
    
*   **Editor**: a member that will be able to **see and edit all files** of your organization.
    
*   **Viewer**: a member that will only be able to **see all files** of your organization.
    

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FQB4mpPb0QI4npRTJwMQl%252FFrame%25201762%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4555e6b4-c852-40e2-a315-06d709068bad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1369e29c&sv=2)

5

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#set-up-your-preferences)

Set up your preferences

You are now done with the onboarding. Choose **a way to navigate in Rayon**...

*   Either using a **mouse** or **trackpad**
    
*   Either using **shortcuts** or the **command line**
    

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252F4xEquMKVRZcXteOmXrUO%252FFrame%25201786%2520%286%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46ef1bee-b6d5-495d-97a2-cd0159b0ff29&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aaed5f87&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up#h_9b5c24fd05-1)

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FTv40r3x5hO3pb0Ga7vL2%252FFrame%25201765%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48a64891-daf7-42f6-aa6c-5a0b7abf27e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3ef5c04&sv=2)

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FbdheUvhV95b7iXejIHYK%252FVincent-F-11%2520%286%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1e15008-abbe-4d1d-ad3c-802255be6045&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5c4cc0f&sv=2)

# Organizations | Rayon Docs 

Rayon is great for **teams** that love to **collaborate**.

To that end, **Rayon** offers **organizations**: a simple way to share [**workspaces**](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/workspaces)
, **models**, **templates** and **libraries** while making sure everyone has appropriate access.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations#organization-setup-and-access)

Organization setup and access

Setting up an organization can be done at signup, or later on, in the project manager context menu. In either case, Rayon will ask you to set a name for your organization and to invite other users.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FLv3kH7EnYvYc9ceAahzm%252FFrame%25201780%2520%285%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46dc4650-f85a-4eb7-b45b-f1ca56d1e85c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed35d61a&sv=2)

In project manager

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FplNDtiNXQy1LgZPG4t5v%252Fimage%2520%281%29.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D590d537e-dadb-4fb2-8dda-97d5a17c7855&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a46b7b5f&sv=2)

During onboarding

The **curation of users** having access to the organization, as well as their **role**, and the **billing** attached to your organization can be managed from the organization's settings page.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252F0N422IkeShI3fQjZwsqb%252FVincent-F-13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93b307f4-9722-49de-9ca9-71e27148ad57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e2f5f8d0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations#h_09b97c1849)

User roles

When inviting users to an organization, it is important to understand their role. Members can have **4 types of roles** in an organization...

Role

View models

Edit models

Set org. settings

Curate org. users

**Owner**

**Admin**

**Editor**

**Viewer**

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations#h_09b97c1849-1)

Billing

Billing in Rayon always happens at the organization level. At any time, the organization's **owner** may...

*   Update their **organization's plan (**[Learn more about Rayon's pricing](https://www.rayon.design/pricing)
    )
    
*   Update the **billing address**
    
*   Download **invoices**
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations#tutorial)

Tutorial

For more step-by-step information, watch our tutorial about how to work as an organization in Rayon:

* * *

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations#we-are-always-available)

. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)

# Exporting & printing | Rayon Docs 

You may **export your model** as **PNG, PDF, DWG, DXF** or **simply send it to your printer.**

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_327a882dca)

Exporting an image

To **export** your **model** as an **image,**

*   Open the `**Pages**` panel.
    
*   Then, click the `**+**` button to **create a new Page.**
    
*   **Select the page frame** on the canvas and resize it to fit your drawing.
    
*   Select `**... > Export > PNG**` in the **Page panel**
    
*   That's it! Your file will is saved in your **Downloads folder.**
    

Alternatively, you can export the whole screen as an image through `**Menu > Export > Image**`

To get more **tips** about **pages**, go to the Pages Documentation.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FsIfr4TOXtNnXWfH1DYGM%252FPreviewer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c63a567-b098-4b42-9512-7db700bce36d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e06be5d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_e7382427ae)

Exporting a PDF file

To **export** your **model** as a **PDF file,**

*   Open the `**Pages**` panel.
    
*   Then, click the `**+**` button to **create a new Page.**
    
*   **Select the Page frame** on the canvas and resize it to fit your drawing.
    
*   (Optional) set your **Page** **scale** in the right panel
    
*   Select `**... > Export > PDF**` in the **Page panel**
    
*   That's it! Your file will is saved in your **Downloads folder.**
    

To get more **tips** about **pages**, go to the Pages Documentation.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_e7382427ae-1)

**Exporting a DWG or DXF**

To **export** your **model** as a **DWG** or **DXF file,**

*   Click on the `**Menu**` button.
    
*   Hover on `**Export**` and choose select `**DWG**` or `**DXF**`.
    
*   Click on the `**Download**` button that appears on top of the editor**.**
    
*   That's it! Your file will is saved in your **Downloads folder.**
    

_Note : When exporting to DWG, the colours of the entities will be based on the colour of the layer they are placed on. More about our_ [_layers_](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/layers)
_._

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_e7382427ae-2)

**Printing**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To **print** your **pages** and send them to your printer...

*   Open the `**Pages**` panel.
    
*   Then, click the `**export**` button button
    
*   In the export modal that opens, select the `**print**` option
    
*   The browser print interface will show up.
    
*   Choose your paper format and printer and press `**print**`.
    

For more step-by-step information, watch our tutorial about how to import & export in Rayon:

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

[PreviousPDF & image import](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/pdf-and-image-import)
[NextPublishing & sharing](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Exporting a PDF file](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_e7382427ae)
    
*   [Exporting a DWG or DXF](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing#h_e7382427ae-1)

# Pricing & billing | Rayon Docs 

Welcome to **Rayon’s pricing guide.** This page explains the different plans, what’s included at each tier, how billing works, and answers common questions.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/pricing-and-billing#pricing-overview)

Pricing overview

Rayon offers a **free plan** and **two paid plans** (Pro and Team). You can choose to pay **monthly** or **yearly** (with a 20% discount for yearly billing). You can also pay in **monthly installments** or as a **yearly lump sum** (with 20% discount).

In Euro (€)

In Dollar ($)

Plan

Price (per editor)

Key Features

**Free**

€0 / $0

• Unlimited models • Async support • Limited PDF/PNG export • Limited access to Rayon libraries • Limited model history

**Pro**

**Monthly** ~€25 / month/per editor **Yearly** ~€19 / month/per editor

Everything in Free, plus: • Full PDF & PNG export • Full access to Rayon libraries • Unlimited model history • Personal templates & libraries • Ability to share models

• Async support

**Team**

**Monthly** ~€45 / month/per editor **Yearly** ~€35 / month/per editor

Everything in Pro, plus: • Team templates & libraries • Team workspaces • Team-level billing • Live support

\*Note: Prices are per editor/account. “Editor” refers to a user who can edit or collaborate on models within your team.

Plan

Price (per editor)

Key Features

**Free**

€0 / $0

• Unlimited models • Async support • Limited PDF/PNG export • Limited access to Rayon libraries • Limited model history

**Pro**

**Monthly** ~$27 / month/per editor **Yearly** ~$21 / month/per editor

Everything in Free, plus: • Full PDF & PNG export • Full access to Rayon libraries • Unlimited model history • Personal templates & libraries • Ability to share models

• Async support

**Team**

**Monthly** ~$49 / month/per editor **Yearly** ~$38 / month/per editor

Everything in Pro, plus: • Team templates & libraries • Team workspaces • Team-level billing • Live support

\*Note: Prices are per editor/account. “Editor” refers to a user who can edit or collaborate on models within your team.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/pricing-and-billing#billing-and-payment)

Billing & payment

*   **Monthly vs Yearly** You may choose to pay monthly or annually. The yearly option gives a discount compared to paying month to month.
    
*   **Per-editor billing** Each paid plan’s cost is tied to the number of editors (users with editing rights). If you add or remove editors, your billing adjusts accordingly.
    
*   **Team billing** On the Team plan, billing is centralized—typically handled by a designated account owner or administrator in your organization.
    
*   **Upgrading / Downgrading** You can upgrade your plan (e.g. from Free → Pro, or Pro → Team) at any time. If you downgrade, features from the higher plan may be disabled or limited after your current billing cycle ends.
    
*   **Cancellation** You can cancel your paid plan at any time. After cancellation, your account will revert to the Free plan at the end of your billing period (or immediately, depending on your policy).
    
*   **Invoices & Receipts** Paid subscribers can get invoices or receipts via the billing dashboard in Stripe. (You may want to specify how and where in your app users access invoices.)
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/pricing-and-billing#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Sharing a model or a workspace | Rayon Docs 

We covered how to **export your work** as **.pdf, .dwg/.dwx** and **.png** in [Exporting models](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing)
.

Here, we describe how to **share** your models **in Rayon**, so that your coworkers can access them right in their browser.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/sharing-a-model-or-a-workspace#sharing-a-workspace)

Sharing a workspace

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252F0pJvzCc8DwsoUNxBZynT%252FVincent-F-7%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b2d6f1f-0639-4fb4-8a79-7dd6680cc041&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d1dd152&sv=2)

By default, new **workspaces** created in an **organization** are accessible to **every member of the organization**. All the **models** inside these **workspaces** are then accessible as well.

You may want to share a workspace with an external person. To do so, access your **workspace settings**, then enter the email address of the person you would like to share your model with.

People can be invited as **Viewer, Editor** or **Admin**. These roles come with certain **rights**, outlined below :

Action

Admin

Editor

Viewer

**View**

**Measure**

**Comment**

**Annotate**

**Edit**

**Delete**

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/sharing-a-model-or-a-workspace#sharing-a-model-to-a-specific-person)

Sharing a model to a specific person

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Fr6UT7xrjW9NMFz2My2TJ%252FVincent-F-7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e73a420-4f41-4adc-a345-930a46efdccb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47a76fba&sv=2)

Click on the **Share** button in the top-right of the editor, then enter the email address of the person you would like to share your model with.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/sharing-a-model-or-a-workspace#sharing-a-model-via-a-public-link)

Sharing a model via a public link

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FSfrGcBekVOdt6lXP46OQ%252FVincent-F-7-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6f0ff24-e10f-4d42-a654-45a65949da56&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50754767&sv=2)

Click on the **Share** button in the top-right of the editor then enter the email address of the person you would like to share your model with.

People will only have access as **Viewer**.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/sharing-a-model-or-a-workspace#tutorial)

Tutorial

For more step-by-step information, watch our tutorial about how to work as an organization in Rayon.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/sharing-a-model-or-a-workspace#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Private and Public Model Settings [Beta] | Rayon Docs 

In Rayon, you can set your models to **Public** or **Private**, depending on your plan.

**Public models** are visible to everyone in the Rayon community. Anyone can view, duplicate, and use them as templates. For Free plan users, all models are Public by default.

**Private models** are hidden from the Rayon community and cannot be accessed or duplicated by others. Only Pro and Team plan users can create Private models.

If you downgrade from a paid plan to the free plan or if your free trial ends, your Private models will remain Private but become **Read-Only**. You can still download them in any format, but editing will only be possible if you switch them to Public or upgrade your plan.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#where-do-i-access-my-models-visibility-settings)

Where do I access my model's visibility settings?

You can toggle on the `Private` or `Public` tabs from your model's top right side property panel:

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMawW0q0oMi7Gkw4NlsyX%252FPreview%2520Presentation.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28f9397b-9eed-469e-baef-35f0039dbf5a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca21e07d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#faq)

FAQ

**I have a Free Rayon account. How does Private/Public mode work?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#i-have-a-free-rayon-account.-how-does-private-public-mode-work)

With a Free account, your models will be Public by default and therefore visible to everyone in the Rayon community. Anyone can view, duplicate, and use them as templates. If you want to set a model to Private, you'd need to upgrade your plan to Pro or Team.

**I have a Pro/Team Rayon account. How does Private/Public mode work?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#i-have-a-pro-team-rayon-account.-how-does-private-public-mode-work)

With a Pro or Team account, you can switch between Private and Public modes. Private models are hidden from the Rayon community and cannot be viewed or duplicated by others.

**I have a Pro/Team account but want to switch to the Free plan. How can I keep my work private?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#i-have-a-pro-team-account-but-want-to-switch-to-the-free-plan.-how-can-i-keep-my-work-private)

If you downgrade to the Free plan, your Private models will remain private but become accessible in Read-Only mode. To edit them again, you can switch them to Public or upgrade your plan. In Read-Only mode, you can still download them as DWG, DXF, PDF, Image, or a Rayon file.

**Note:** Private and Public modes are currently in Beta. If you don’t see this option in your account, all of your models are set to Private by default.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Rayon for universities | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMrYJyUlWsULknbwwhWLv%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49fd0779-4b8d-4af0-bbbe-74455655e713&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=af6ef939&sv=2)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#rayon-is-the-best-online-cad-software-enabling-faculty-and-students-to-teach-and-learn-architecture)

Rayon is the best online CAD software, enabling faculty and students to teach and learn architecture/interior design in a modern, collaborative platform. Rayon is free for the academic world, and offers a _student plan_ for individuals (students, faculty, instructors) and an _academia plan_ for institutions, to offer more control, security and university-level features.


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#what-is-rayon)

What is Rayon?

Rayon is an **online, collaborative software for architects, interior designers**, etc allowing users to draft, stylise and present their work. It is a one-stop-solution to create complete drawing sets. More importantly, Rayon is **a professional CAD tool**, that offers the full depth that is typical to well known drawing software in the AEC. Rayon is **an ideal platform for teaching and learning architecture and interior design**, and is adopted by 150k+ student around the world.

Here are some useful links to discover Rayon...

*   [Rayon 20 minute demo](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B2kc4kXJrkA)
    
*   [Rayon's website](https://rayon.design/)
    
*   [Rayon's signup page](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#why-set-up-rayon-for-your-university)

Why set up Rayon for your university?

Our hope by opening the software for free to faculty and instructors is **to finally offer a collaborative CAD environment that provides architecture and interior architecture/design curriculums the means teach with a modern tool set**.

*   **For students** — Rayon provides students with hands-on experience in a modern, professional CAD design tool. Rayon blends together the full spectrum of important software features (drafting, stylising, layout), and is compatible with exiting legacy software (AutoCAD/Rhino etc through DWG import/export, and SketchUp using Rayon's dedicated plugin)
    
*   **For faculty** — Rayon empowers faculty with a collaborative software, where they can easily to manage class projects, set up CAD class material, receive students submission and provide feedbacks, all in one place.
    
*   **For universities** — Rayon is the ideal offering to help university support their community, with minimum setup and maintenance cost. Rayon helps...
    
    *   Simplify software setup with a browser-based platform accessible from any device, with no install.
        
    *   Encourage teamwork and peer learning through shared workspaces.
        
    *   Ensure secure oversight with full admin rights for institutional IT or academic staff.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#academia-plan-key-features)

Academia plan key features

To apply, [fill in the form right here.](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/YnkcFT25#source=docs)

The Academia Plan provides academic institutions with the same benefits as Rayon's **Team Plan**, to support teaching and research. It allows faculty to create shared workspaces, run classes, and collaborate with students in real time — all within a browser-based platform that requires no installation.

Among other things, the academia plan encompasses....

*   **Full Team Plan** Universities and schools receive a full Team plan. Students are added to shared workspaces where they can collaborate, learn, and build projects together.
    
*   **Faculty Accounts** Professors and teaching staff can run classes, organize projects, and guide students in a multiplayer drafting environment.
    
*   **Full Admin Access** University administrators have complete control over the institution’s account, including user management, permissions, and workspace organization.
    
*   **Teaching-Ready Platform** Designed for design studios, architecture courses, and other project-based classes, Rayon supports collaborative drafting, feedback, and presentation. Faculty can publish templates and give students access to tailored made resources.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#how-to-apply)

How to Apply

The Academia Plan is available to universities, colleges and academic institutions. To apply...

1.  Faculty and university admins can contact our support team [by filing this form](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/YnkcFT25#source=docs)
    .
    
2.  Our team onboards them in a 15-minute call, and set up free credentials for their institution.
    
3.  Enrolled students and faculty get free team-level access to all of Rayon's feature set.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#faq)

FAQ

Is Rayon free for students, faculty and university?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#is-rayon-free-for-students-faculty-and-university)

**Yes it is!** By default, students, and faculty signing to Rayon with their academic email will get a student plan account for free (the equivalent of our Pro pan). On top of that, we constantly add new universities to our **academia plan** (the equivalent of our Team pan). If your university is in, then **your students and faculty will be grouped together inside the same school organization**, carrying the name of your institution. This way they will be able to share repositories of models together, which is ideally to teach and collaborate as a class. If you think your university should be part of the academia plan, [then reach out to us here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/YnkcFT25#source=docs)
.

If my university is on the academia plan, how do students/faculty join the university organization?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#if-my-university-is-on-the-academia-plan-how-do-students-faculty-join-the-university-organization)

It is automatic; all existing student or prospective ones will be automatically added to your university organization if it exists. You don't need to do anything.

How can faculty ensure their class material remains secure?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#how-can-faculty-ensure-their-class-material-remains-secure)

Within a school organization, models are grouped into workspaces. These are likely public folders that any member of the university can access.

However, when it comes to teaching classes, faculty often require a bit more privacy. This where **private workspaces** are so useful. A private workspace is a folder that belongs to its creator, and onto which selected users can be invited. With a private workspace, faculty can easily prepare some class content, and then invite certain students to join the folder.

How do we know our school data is safe?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#how-do-we-know-our-school-data-is-safe)

We are f**ully GDPR-compliant**, which ensures ...

*   **Lawful basis for processing** We have a valid legal reason to collect and user's personal data (e.g., consent, contract, legitimate interest, legal obligation).
    
*   **Transparency & notice** We clearly explain which data we collect, why, who we share it with, and how long we keep it.
    
*   **Data minimization** We collect only the data we truly need for our stated purpose.
    
*   **Accuracy** We keep personal data up to date and correct inaccuracies.
    
*   **Storage limitation** We don't keep personal data longer than necessary.
    
*   **Integrity & confidentiality** We secure data (technical and organizational measures — e.g., encryption, access controls).
    
*   **Accountability** We can prove our compliance if audited (records of processing activities, contracts with processors, DPIAs if needed).
    

Can models contained inside our school organization be shared with external people?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#can-models-contained-inside-our-school-organization-be-shared-with-external-people)

No. Any model or workspace contained inside your university organization will be only accessible to people from your school/university.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

*   [Why set up Rayon for your university?](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#why-set-up-rayon-for-your-university)
    
*   [Academia plan key features](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-universities#academia-plan-key-features)

# System requirements | Rayon Docs 

Rayon is an online software. Although we provide [an installed app](https://www.rayon.design/download)
, it is common to use Rayon directly in the browser.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/system-requirements#supported-browsers)

**Supported browsers**

Rayon supports mainstream browser, up until a certain legacy version, for each browser. We list here the cut-off, for each one.

*   **Chrome**: 119+
    
*   **Opera**: 105+
    
*   **Firefox**: 118+
    
*   **Edge**: 119+
    

We recommend updating your browser, to benefit from the best experience when using Rayon.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/system-requirements#browsers-not-supported)

**Browsers not supported**

*   **Safari**: unfortunately, Safari is suffering from a known issue with apps like ours, using multithreading and web assembly. We cannot support Safari until this issue gets resolved.
    
*   **Internet Explorer**
    
*   **Safari for iOS**
    
*   **Android browser**
    

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/system-requirements#internet-connection)

Internet connection

Rayon requires an internet connection to start working. Only with in internet connection can the app be loaded on your computer, be it your browser or in the installed app. Once loaded, Rayon can be used offline. All that matters is that you are connected to the internet again before closing or refreshing the tab you are working on.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/system-requirements#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

[PreviousSupport](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
[NextRefund policy](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Rayon for students | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Fy2a6Y92dPhgW1oHPGtDr%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De28c8c3d-5d23-4654-864f-40e4b2569d02&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65f088a0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#rayon-is-the-best-online-cad-software-enabling-faculty-and-students-to-teach-and-learn-architecture)

Rayon is the best online CAD software, enabling faculty and students to teach and learn architecture/interior design in a modern, collaborative platform. Rayon is **free for students from accredited institutions!**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To set up your account, you can create your **free student account** [**at this link.**](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    
*   If you institution is not accredited, [**simply feel in this form.**](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/d9WNl3bl#source=docs)
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#what-is-rayon)

What is Rayon?

Rayon is an **online, collaborative software for architects, interior designers**, etc allowing users to draft, stylise and present their work. It is a one-stop-solution to create complete drawing sets. More importantly, Rayon is **a professional CAD tool**, that offers the full depth that is typical to well known drawing software in the AEC.

Here are some useful links to discover Rayon...

*   [Rayon 20 minute demo](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B2kc4kXJrkA)
    
*   [Rayon's website](https://rayon.design/)
    
*   [Rayon's signup page](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#why-use-rayon-us-rayon-to-study)

Why use Rayon us Rayon to study?

Our hope by opening the software for free to students is **to finally offer a collaborative CAD environment that provides young architecture and interior architecture/design practitioners the means to learn teach in a modern tool set**.

As a professional CAD environment that supports multiplayer editing and reviewing, Rayon is essentially **the ideally platform to gather architecture/interior design students,** and is adopted by 150k+ of them around the world.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#account-creation)

Account creation

To get a student account, please follow these few steps:

*   Create a Rayon account, [at this link](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    , using an academic institutional email. Note that generic emails (like gmail, hotmail, etc.) will not be eligible for a student account.
    
*   During the onboarding, when asked, please don't forget to select the ‘I am a student’ option.
    
    *   **If your school is already in our student program**, then you will automatically be set on the student plan.
        
    *   **If your school is not yet in our student program**, and you declared in the onboarding that you were a student, then you will receive a form by email, a few minutes after signing up, allowing you to submit your application to get a student plan. If you are validated, we will bump you to our student plan, and add your university to our list of partner universities. This way, all students signing up to Rayon after you will receive automatically a student status.
        
    
*   **Your student plan will give you access to all the features of our Pro plan**: watermark-less exports, access to Rayon's entire libraries, etc.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#faq)

FAQ

Questions students usually ask, answers we usually give!

**Is my school accredited already?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#is-my-school-accredited-already)

To know, simply create a Rayon account using your institutional email, and choose the "student/faculty" option in the onboarding. If your school is accredited, you will receive a validation email right after the end of your onboarnding, confirming that you have been granted a student account

**My university does not provide students with institutional emails. Can I send you my student ID for proof?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#my-university-does-not-provide-students-with-institutional-emails.-can-i-send-you-my-student-id-for)

Unfortunately, no. Non-institutional emails (like Gmail, Hotmail, etc.) will not be eligible for a student account.

**I created a Rayon account, but I did not mention I am a student in the onboarding. How can I fix this?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#i-created-a-rayon-account-but-i-did-not-mention-i-am-a-student-in-the-onboarding.-how-can-i-fix-this)

That should not be a problem; even if you did not take the right step during the onboarding, you should have received a free student plan if your institution is accredited.

**My school gave me an alumni email; can I use it to get a student plan?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#my-school-gave-me-an-alumni-email-can-i-use-it-to-get-a-student-plan)

Unfortunately, no. We only grant a student plan to active/enrolled students. Alumni email are therefore not accepted.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Rayon for studying | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FavWiJ8uDQKxSP1NiqdUu%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e472f87-eafe-4a8e-aa4a-1763442701d8&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bbdad2c&sv=2)

**Rayon is free for the academic world.**

Our hope by opening the software for free to students, faculty and universities at large is **to finally offer a collaborative CAD environment that provides architecture and interior architecture/design curriculums the means to learn and teach with a modern tool set**. As a professional CAD environment that supports multiplayer editing and reviewing, Rayon is essentially the ideally platform to gather architecture/interior design students and faculty.

Today, Rayon offers free accounts to students and faculty through its _**student plan.**_ Rayon also offers more control to academic institutions (admin rights, SSO, repository curation, etc), thanks to its _**academic plan**_. Both are free, and can be explored below.

To get started, **click on the option below that best represents who you are...**

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-students)

![Cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Fc57jzliCrXvAUuDzmroU%252FGroup%252099249989.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0cbb1bdd-115f-461a-8944-39b4b078b3f7&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9b244b4&sv=2)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty)

# Rayon for faculty | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252F5jHL3xdqn3q2IeyO2HPL%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38e02b46-fb2f-4eed-b683-a6bb7f62caa1&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a8777460&sv=2)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#rayon-is-the-best-online-cad-software-enabling-faculty-and-students-to-teach-and-learn-architecture)

Rayon is the best online CAD software, enabling faculty and students to teach and learn architecture/interior design in a modern, collaborative platform. Rayon is **free for students from accredited institutions!**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To set up your account, you can create your **free faculty account** [**at this link.**](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    
*   If your institution is not accredited, [**simply feel in this form.**](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/d9WNl3bl#source=docs)
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#what-is-rayon)

What is Rayon?

Rayon is an **online, collaborative software for architects, interior designers**, etc allowing users to draft, stylise and present their work. It is a one-stop-solution to create complete drawing sets. More importantly, Rayon is **a professional CAD tool**, that offers the full depth that is typical to well known drawing software in the AEC.

Here are some useful links to discover Rayon...

*   [Rayon 20-minute demo](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B2kc4kXJrkA)
    
*   [Rayon's website](https://rayon.design/)
    
*   [Rayon's signup page](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#why-use-rayon-to-teach)

Why use Rayon to teach?

Our hope by opening the software for free to faculty and instructors is **to finally offer a collaborative CAD environment that provides architecture and interior architecture/design curriculums the means to teach with a modern tool set**.

As a professional CAD environment that supports multiplayer editing and reviewing, Rayon is essentially **the ideal platform to gather architecture/interior design students,** and is adopted by 150k+ students around the world.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#how-does-rayon-work)

How does Rayon work?

**1) Start simple: create an account**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#id-1-start-simple-create-an-account)

*   Rayon is simpler to access than legacy software; all you need is a browser.
    
*   To get started, you can [create an account right here](https://rayon.design/app/auth/student-signup)
    .
    
*   Everything about Rayon signup steps [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up)
    .
    

**Tip** — We recommend you install our native app, to access Rayon faster. [Download page here](https://www.rayon.design/download)
.

**2) Work with the data you already have: DWG / CTB / PDF, etc**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#id-2-work-with-the-data-you-already-have-dwg-ctb-pdf-etc)

*   **Rayon allows you to work with the files you already have** (DWG, PDFs, Images).
    
*   **DWG** can be read entirely. Rayon transposes their entire layer structure, blocks, hatch files etc. Import is lossless, making you feel like you started within a CAD software you already know.
    
*   **CTBs** can be entirely replicated easily in Rayon, by using Rayon's styles. More on this [topic right here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)
    .
    

**3) Draft like you know how**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#id-3-draft-like-you-know-how)

*   **Drawing habits from legacy CAD softwares translate in Rayon, to make you feel at home:** Rayon works with a command line, tools can be called using shortcuts, drawing are organised with layers, etc.
    
*   Everything about Rayon's design experience [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design)
    .
    

**4) Prepare your class' content**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#id-4-prepare-your-class-content)

*   Models you make can be shared with students by inviting them as co-editors. [More about sharing ability here.](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/sharing-commenting-annotating#h_f9c38d116b-1)
    
*   Models can also be turned into templates to facilitate sharing them to your class. Also, your students can be gathered in a shared repository (a workspace), where they can deposit their work. These features are part of the _academia_ plan, for which your university needs to apply if it is not part of our program already. [Please submit this form](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/YnkcFT25#source=docs)
     to give your school access to Rayon's full scope of sharing features.
    
*   Everything about libraries and templates [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/publishing-a-library)
    .
    

**5) Chat and offer feedbacks**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#id-5-chat-and-offer-feedbacks)

*   Rayon is a **multiplayer software**.
    
*   It is the first software for architects that finally brings live co-editing to design teams.
    
*   Additionally, Rayon allows you to comment/annotate your work, to make sure your team stays in sync.
    
*   Everything about Rayon's collaborative layer [can be found at this link](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/sharing-commenting-annotating)
    .
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#faq)

FAQ

Questions faculty usually ask, answers we usually give!

**Is my school/university accredited already?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#is-my-school-university-accredited-already)

To know, simply create a Rayon account using your institutional email, and choose the "student/faculty" option in the onboarding. If your school is accredited, you will receive a validation email right after the end of your onboarding, confirming that you have been granted a student account.

**My university does not provide faculty with institutional emails. Can I send you my student ID for proof?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#my-university-does-not-provide-faculty-with-institutional-emails.-can-i-send-you-my-student-id-for-p)

Unfortunately, no. Non-institutional emails (like Gmail, Hotmail, etc.) will not be eligible for a faculty account.

**I created a Rayon account, but I did not mention I am a faculty in the onboarding. How can I fix this?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#i-created-a-rayon-account-but-i-did-not-mention-i-am-a-faculty-in-the-onboarding.-how-can-i-fix-this)

That should not be a problem; even if you did not take the right step during the onboarding, you should have received a free student plan if your institution is accredited.

**My school gave me an alumni email; can I use it to get a student plan?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/rayon-for-studying/rayon-for-faculty#my-school-gave-me-an-alumni-email-can-i-use-it-to-get-a-student-plan)

Unfortunately, no. We only grant a faculty plan to active/enrolled faculty. Alumni email are therefore not accepted.

# Support | Rayon Docs 

At Rayon, we do our best to **offer our users the best support experience**. We detail in this page this support experience entails.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#support-resources)

Support resources

More generally, support happens by **various means and resources.** We list here all these resources:

*   **In-person support**: through our in-app chat panel, for `**Pro**` and `**Team**` plan level users
    
*   **Community support**: our community website allows any user to get help from our community manager or from the community itself. [Its website can be found here.](https://community.rayon.design/)
    
*   **Support resources** (available to all users):
    
    *   **Tutorials**: our academy, containing ore than 100 hours of training material, [can be found here](https://academy.rayon.design/)
        .
        
    *   **Documentation**: our documentation [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)
        .
        
    *   `**soon**` **AI-panel**: we will offer as of December 2025 an in-app AI panel, allowing all users to be support by an AI assistant.
        
    
*   **Demos & Webinars**: we offer demos and webinars to our users, where they can join to learn Rayon's best practices, and get answers to their questions. The link to book a time slot [can be found right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
    .
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#plan-vs-support-policy)

Plan vs support policy

Support level is tied to the user's plan. We specify below what can be expected...

Plan

Weekdays support

Weekends support

**Free**

No in-person support

No in-person support

**Student**

No in-person support

No in-person support

**Pro**

In-person async support (Avg. answer time : 3 to 5 h.\*)

No in-person support

**Team**

In-person live support (Avg. answer time : 5 min.\*)

No in-person support

(\*) Answer time is subject to support opening hours; our support staff is available from 9 AM to 6 PM CET. Answer time specified above applies during these time slots. Messages received on weekdays outside these time slots will be answered as soon as our service reopens the next day.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#faq)

FAQ

Some question relating to support...

I emailed your support; should I expect an answer?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#i-emailed-your-support-should-i-expect-an-answer)

Rayon only supports Team plan users by email. Free, Pro, and Student plan users can get support in-app only.

I am a `**free**`/`**student**` plan user; how can I get some support?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#i-am-a-free-student-plan-user-how-can-i-get-some-support)

Rayon offers **1-on-1 support to paying users only**. However, there are other ways to get some support:

*   [Join our community](https://community.rayon.design/)
     and get some help from our community manager or from the community itself.
    
*   You can use our resources ([Tutorials](https://academy.rayon.design/)
    , [Docs](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)
    , etc).
    
*   You can [join a demo or webinar](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
    .
    
*   You can use our AI-panel to get some immediate help.
    

I am on the free plan, but have a question regarding upgrading my team to a paid plan; how can I get in touch with someone at Rayon?[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#i-am-on-the-free-plan-but-have-a-question-regarding-upgrading-my-team-to-a-paid-plan-how-can-i-get-i)

**We can help you upgrade any time**. If you are still on a free plan, and want some help to upgrade, email us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

If you are on the `**Pro**` plan or `**Team**` plan, simply message our support reps in the in-app support panel.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.
