# Creating zoning plans in Rayon | Rayon Docs 

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#what-is-a-zoning-plan)

What is a zoning plan?

A zoning plan is a foundational drawing that defines the **permitted use, placement, and size of a development** in accordance with local zoning regulations. It typically shows property boundaries, allowed building areas, and designated land uses.

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FJIUPixokFkMpbgj07Ixk%252FPreviewer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D528bb9c8-8e3e-4f78-87cc-13c242e04d3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6742d88a&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#how-to-create-a-zoning-plan-in-rayon)

How to create a zoning plan in Rayon?

Creating a zoning plan in Rayon typically takes between 1 and 2 hours, depending on the property's size and complexity. To get started, all you’ll need is a **DWG or PDF of the property**, along with information about the local rules and regulations relevant to your development.

🔗 Here is a link to [Rayon's Zoning Template](https://www.rayon.design/app/model/f510f416-1e4d-485e-9f76-8c9506b2fd46?canvas=V3VmgEPTVp2&scale=1189.1244713620945&x=184933803.93246838&y=21285201.191463083&token=rayon-template)
. Let's get started!

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#id-1-import-your-drawing-5-minutes)

(1) Import your drawing: _5 minutes_

Importing drawings in Rayon is easy.

*   Select the `Import DWG/PDF` from the main menu of your model.
    
*   Rayon will ask you to asses the scale of your drawing.
    

Read more about importing [here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/dwg-dxf-import)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#id-2-draw-a-legend-5-minutes)

**(2) Draw a legend:** _**5 minutes**_

Draw a legend that lists permitted uses and building placement, and format it according to your local drafting standards.

*   Use the `Rectangle` tool, then select it and set its `Style` from the right-side panel. There, you can set a color, hatch, line type, and more. Then **save and name your style** to use moving forward.
    
*   Use the `Text` tool to add descriptions to your legend.
    

Read more about Styles [here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)
.

**(3) Draw zones:** _**15-30 minutes**_

Rayon's `Zone` tool offers two ways to define areas:

*   **Polyline Zone:** Use the `Zone` tool to draw a closed shape. Its tag will **display the area in square meters**, updating as you adjust the shape.
    
*   **Zone within a wall enclosure:** First, draw `walls` to enclose an area on your floor plan. Then, use the `Zone` to fill that enclosed space **with a simple click**. The surface will display a **square meter tag** that updates as the enclosure is modified.
    

Read more about the zone tool [here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/elements-walls-zones-openings-etc)
.

**(4) Create a Zoning table:** _**15-20 minutes**_

Let’s list, count, and sum your zones quickly with Rayon’s table tool!

*   **Name zones** by selecting them and editing their `Name` property.
    
*   Add **metadata** to your zones for smart scheduling. For example, you can add to each zone a `Category` metadata property to group designated land use (like Public, Commercial, and Residential).
    

*   **Create a table** listing zones according to their category by:
    
    *   Generating a new table from the `+` button
        
    *   Enabling the `zone` category only
        
    *   Adding the `Area` and `Category` properties
        
    *   Grouping your table according to `Category`
        
    *   You now have a schedule that includes each zone name, category, and SQM, along with their total count and sum. `Export` it to an Excel sheet!
        
    
    Read more about Tables here.
    

**(5) Share your work:** _**5 minutes**_

You’ve reached the last step! Now that you have your architectural zoning plan and a table with data, arrange them as `pages` and `share` directly from Rayon **with a URL link**.

*   `Import` your table in PDF format and place it next to your architectural drawing.
    
*   Place a `page` on your canvas and set its **scale and paper size**.
    
*   Add a **title block** from Rayon’s `block library` and customize it.
    
*   **Share your work** as a URL link by clicking the `Share` button and copying the URL. Now send it to stakeholders!
    

Read more about Pages here.

And…. That’s it! You completed the five steps of creating a zoning plan in Rayon. Feel free to customize and use [Rayon's Zoning Template](https://www.rayon.design/app/model/f510f416-1e4d-485e-9f76-8c9506b2fd46?canvas=V3VmgEPTVp2&scale=1189.1244713620945&x=184933803.93246838&y=21285201.191463083&token=rayon-template)
 for your own projects! 🔗

For more step-by-step information, watch our full tutorial about how to create a zoning plan in Rayon:

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

[PreviousPrivate and Public Model Settings \[Beta\]](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/private-and-public-model-settings-beta)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [What is a zoning plan?](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#what-is-a-zoning-plan)
    
*   [How to create a zoning plan in Rayon?](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#how-to-create-a-zoning-plan-in-rayon)
    
*   [We are always available](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/creating-zoning-plans-in-rayon#we-are-always-available)

# FAQ | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FNxqNyOlZWLbiYS1taXFP%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4afa4075-b99f-4ed1-ba0f-2be3d5043f74&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=726814d7&sv=2)

Cannot find an answer to your question? Then consider [joining our community](https://community.rayon.design/)
!

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#about-using-rayon)

About using Rayon

**I want to change the units of the plan I imported. How do I do that?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#i-want-to-change-the-units-of-the-plan-i-imported.-how-do-i-do-that)

Nothing is simpler! Units can be edited in the settings of your model's canvases directly. More on this topic in our [settings page.](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/setup)

**Why does the lines' thicknesses look different when I export my model to PNG/PDF?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#why-does-the-lines-thicknesses-look-different-when-i-export-my-model-to-png-pdf)

Both the **Stroke scale** property and at the **Page scale** property impact the appearance of lines at export. Here's [detailed documentation about it.](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/setup)

**I cannot find the furniture I need in Rayon’s libraries. How can I get other types of furniture?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#i-cannot-find-the-furniture-i-need-in-rayons-libraries.-how-can-i-get-other-types-of-furniture)

Don't worry. We got you covered!

Rayon has built an entire repository of more than 10k+ furniture blocks called 'Rayon assets' that [can be found right here](https://www.rayon.design/assets/libraries)
. Any furniture or collection of furniture can be downloaded from the website and uploaded to Rayon to be used!

**I imported an image of a plan. How can I set it to the right scale?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#i-imported-an-image-of-a-plan.-how-can-i-set-it-to-the-right-scale)

Simply use the `**Scale**` tool.

**Can I share styles across my drawings?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-i-share-styles-across-my-drawings)

You can use **style libraries** or **templates** to that effect. [See our documentation here for more details.](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/publishing-a-template)

**Can I export a PDF/DWG/PNG with Rayon?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-i-export-a-pdf-dwg-png-with-rayon)

Yes! Please have a look at the [Export page](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/exporting-and-printing)
 to learn more about it!

**Which formats can I import into Rayon?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#which-formats-can-i-import-into-rayon)

PDF, DWG, DXF, and images (JPG and PNG) can be imported into Rayon.

There are a few limitations on file sizes; check out our [Import page](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/import-export/dwg-dxf-import)
 for more details.

**Can I copy from one model to another?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-i-copy-from-one-model-to-another)

Yes, absolutely! Simply use the `**Copy as Export**` option. You will find it in the right-click (or by pressing `**CTRL**` + `**SHIFT**` + `**C**`)...then simply paste in the destination model.

**Is Rayon a 3D software?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#is-rayon-a-3d-software)

No, Rayon is a 2D drawing tool only.

**Where can I find doors in Rayon?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#where-can-i-find-doors-in-rayon)

Doors can be found in the block library. [More about block libraries here.](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/publishing-a-library)

**Does Rayon support languages other than English?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#does-rayon-support-languages-other-than-english)

We started offering translations of our app. So far, Rayon offers a French version only, but our team is working on shipping other languages soon.

**How can I swap the email of my account?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#how-can-i-swap-the-email-of-my-account)

Rayon does not offer this option today. The solution is to invite your other email to your organization, and then transfer ownership to this new email.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#about-issues-and-bugs)

About issues & bugs

**My imported DWG is not at the right scale. What can I do?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#my-imported-dwg-is-not-at-the-right-scale.-what-can-i-do)

An imported plan can sometimes be out of scale. This is often caused by a **mismatch between the units** of the original DWG file and Rayon’s unit system.

**For instance, one can be in millimeters and the other in meters.** It is, therefore, just a matter of applying a x1000 factor or x0.0001 to set the drawing back to its original size.

To restore the right scale, simply use the `**Scale**` tool.

**I seem to have lost some models. What can I do?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#i-seem-to-have-lost-some-models.-what-can-i-do)

Losing models is not possible in Rayon. However, Rayon offers different ways to store models (public/private workspaces, folders, etc), and is inherently a collaborative software. For those reasons, we have realized that, sometimes, users misplace models or move them without notifying other users using the same repository. Our advice is to (1) check all repositories you own or are a part too, as well as (2) make sure your colleagues informed you of models they moved or deleted.

**I seem to have lost some part of my drawing. What can I do?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#i-seem-to-have-lost-some-part-of-my-drawing.-what-can-i-do)

The integrity of your work is our #1 priority. In 99% of cases, data will be safely handled. However, on extremely rare occasion (file closed without syncing back to the server, clashes between multiplayer edits, etc), data can get lost. In such situation, first make sure your data is truly lost. (1) Check your model history, and try to revert to previous (more complete) versions. (2) Download your current model (in .ry format) and then refresh the tab. If you’ve tried the above and your data is still not there, please contact our support team ([\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
) — we’ll help you get it resolved quickly. Though we cannot retrieve unsaved work, we can investigate what went wrong.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#about-billing-and-pricing)

About billing & pricing

**How much does Rayon cost?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#how-much-does-rayon-cost)

Rayon is free for a limited usage, or for students. Pricing tiers of our Pro and Team plan can [be found here](https://www.rayon.design/pricing)
.

**How can I cancel my subscription?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#how-can-i-cancel-my-subscription)

To cancel your subscription, please go to Rayon's main menu > settings > billing, and update your plan.

**How can I obtain a refund?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#how-can-i-obtain-a-refund)

Rayon can, under specific conditions, grant some users a refund. [Please see our policy at this page.](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy)

**How can I get an invoice?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#how-can-i-get-an-invoice)

Rayon uses Stripe for billing. Stripe can be accessed from your organization billing page. Withing Stripe, invoices can be generated for any payment you made.

**My payment failed; what can I do?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#my-payment-failed-what-can-i-do)

Payments can sometimes fail for a few reasons (expired card, insufficient funds, bank security checks, etc.). Here’s what you can try:

1.  **Check your card details** Make sure the card number, expiration date, CVC, and billing address are correct and up to date.
    
2.  **Try another card or payment method** If your bank declined the charge, using a different card or payment option often solves the issue.
    
3.  **Contact your bank** Some banks block online or international charges by default. A quick call to approve the payment can fix it.
    
4.  **Update your payment method in your account**
    
    *   Log in to your \[Billing/Account Settings\]
        
    *   Go to **Payment Methods** and add or update your card
        
    *   Retry the payment
        
    

If you’ve tried the above and your payment is still failing, please contact our support team ([\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
) — we’ll help you get it resolved quickly.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#about-system-requirements)

About system requirements

**Can Rayon be used with tablets and smartphones?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-rayon-be-used-with-tablets-and-smartphones)

No, not yet; this feature is in our roadmap but, for the time being, Rayon cannot be used with tablets and smartphones. Though the app can be accessed on these devices, the user experience has not yet been built for it.

**Can Rayon be used offline?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-rayon-be-used-offline)

**Rayon cannot be loaded offline.** However, we do offer the ability to keep working while your connection is lost. Changes done to your model will be synced once you are back online.

**Can I install Rayon on my laptop?**[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#can-i-install-rayon-on-my-laptop)

Yes — although Rayon is first and foremost a webapp, accessible in your browser, Rayon offers an app that can be installed (on PC and Mac alike). This app however does preclude you from needing an internet connection to start Rayon. [This app be downloaded here.](https://www.rayon.design/download)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/faq#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Refund policy | Rayon Docs 

At Rayon, we strive to provide a reliable and high-quality design software experience. We understand that sometimes, specific situations may require a refund or subscription adjustment. **This document outlines the conditions under which refunds are granted**, and when they are not applicable.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#valid-reasons-for-refund)

Valid reasons for refund

We understand that genuine mistakes or technical issues can happen. Refunds may be granted in the following specific circumstances:

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#id-1.-major-technical-issue-reproducible-bug)

1\. Major Technical Issue (Reproducible Bug)

If you experience a significant technical malfunction that prevents normal use of the software, and:

*   The issue is reproducible and confirmed by our technical team.
    
*   Our support team has been informed, and the issue persists despite troubleshooting.
    

In such cases, we will assess the situation and, if applicable, offer a refund or credit.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#id-2.-mistaken-yearly-subscription-payment)

2\. Mistaken Yearly Subscription Payment

If you intended to purchase a monthly subscription but accidentally completed payment for a yearly subscription, we can assist, provided that:

*   You notify our support team within 4 weeks of the purchase date.
    
*   You have not extensively used the software during that period (evaluated at our discretion).
    

In this scenario, we can convert your yearly subscription to a monthly plan and refund the difference.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#id-3.-student-discount-eligibility)

3\. Student Discount Eligibility

Rayon offers free access to enrolled students. If you:

*   Purchased a paid plan while being eligible for a free student license.
    
*   Provide valid proof of active enrolment, such as an institutional email address.
    

We will refund the current month's payment upon verification. Please note that refunds do not apply retroactively beyond the current billing cycle.

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#id-4.-double-charge)

4\. Double Charge

You have encountered the situation where our system has billed you twice; though it is really rare, it can happen, and we would of course pay you back, if you can send us proof of payments.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#non-eligible-reasons-for-refund)

Non-eligible reasons for refund

To maintain fairness and operational clarity, the following situations are not considered valid reasons for refund or subscription cancellation:

*   Lack of Usage: Not using your Rayon account does not qualify for a refund. Subscriptions renew automatically unless cancelled, regardless of usage frequency.
    
*   Auto Renewal: Subscriptions renew automatically unless cancelled. As stated during the upgrade process, cancellation must be completed before the renewal date to avoid being charged. Late cancellations or unawareness of the auto-renewal policy do not qualify for a refund.
    
*   Preference-Based Dissatisfaction: Deciding that you simply "don't like" the software, or finding that it does not match personal preferences after purchase, is not grounds for a refund.
    
*   Changing Needs or Project Status: If your projects change, are cancelled, or you no longer need Rayon, these are not considered valid reasons for a refund.
    
*   Third-Party Expectations: Refunds will not be issued based on comparisons with other software or unmet expectations based on external reviews.
    
*   Plan switch: Refunds will not be offered for users wanting to switch from yearly to monthly plans.
    

We strongly encourage all users to explore our offering and feature set before committing to a paid plan to ensure Rayon meets your needs.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#how-to-request-a-refund)

How to request a refund

To request a refund under the eligible scenarios outlined above:

1.  Contact our support team at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#91e2e4e1e1fee3e5d1e3f0e8feffbff5f4e2f8f6ff)
     or reach out to us through the app support chat.
    
2.  Provide relevant details such as:
    

*   Your registered email address.
    
*   Description of the issue or refund reason.
    
*   Any required proof (e.g., institutional email for student verification).
    

1.  Our team will review your request and respond within 5 business days.
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#final-notes)

Final notes

*   Refunds are issued to the original payment method.
    
*   We reserve the right to decline refund requests that fall outside the conditions stated above.
    
*   We encourage all users to review our pricing, and support resources before committing to a paid plan. More at rayon.design/pricing
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/refund-policy#we-are-always-available)

We are always available

Book a demo with our team, [right here](https://b1kzip68v9f.typeform.com/to/Hgr0eQ4k#source=docs)
. To get some support, reach out to us through our **in-app support chat**. More about [our support policy right here](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/support)
.

# Switching to Rayon | Rayon Docs 

You just discovered Rayon, and you wonder **how to switch** from your previous software (AutoCAD, VectorWorks, Rhinoceros, etc) to us? Then **this page is for you!**

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/switching-to-rayon#what-is-rayon)

What is Rayon?

**Rayon is the fastest CAD software for designing spaces**, working solo or as a team.

Rayon helps today **1000+** companies in **120+ countries**, from the early phase of the design process, all the way to the construction and procurement phases, and beyond.

Rayon is the software for both the **experts** of the built world (architects, interior designers, urbanist, engineer, etc.) and **for all others** (brokers, real estate agents, construction managers, etc.).

To **switch to Rayon**, feel free to visit any of the rubrics below...

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/switching-to-rayon#why-do-teams-switch-to-rayon)

![Cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Ft0cIwMICETezzhu5epzU%252Fshortcuts%2520%285%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d134301-9bca-4652-bbbf-9479a3969d64&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d884bd2&sv=2)

Why do teams switch to Rayon?

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/switching-to-rayon#who-else-is-switching-today)

![Cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252Fo83bebBLcxEfjSYhrvKI%252Fshortcuts-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D902512e6-a6f5-4827-a2f3-d358e8676b75&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1320ef2&sv=2)

Who else is switching today?

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/switching-to-rayon#how-does-switching-work)

![Cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FwDZzU1lc8aeW50i4B6tb%252Fshortcuts-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dc9205b-b80d-4d44-b223-7112b9eba290&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34512063&sv=2)

How does switching work?

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/switching-to-rayon#why-do-teams-switch-to-rayon)

Why do teams switch to Rayon?

**Mainly because the legacy CAD software suffer from clear shortcomings…**

*   **They were not crafted for teams to work together.** Built for desktop, single player, file-based systems: this generation of software simply cannot help modern teams deliver together.
    
*   **They failed to gather the must-have mediums of the trade in a single place**. Architecture is not just lines and shapes: it is also the assembly of building elements, the patchwork of images on a mood board, the meticulous curation of schedules, the compounding of information from the SKU of a single bolt, etc.
    
*   **They were crafted for a small fringe of trained experts…and that is it.** The built world is so much wider than a handful of people needing convoluted, extremely technical solutions. It is a world that still awaits a straightforward, modern and well-rounded solution to craft buildings.
    

The legacy CAD softwares of this world have not delivered the change that our industry hoped for. **Rayon is that change...**

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/switching-to-rayon#who-else-is-switching-today)

Who else is switching today?

Rayon is the new way of designing buildings, **chosen by 1000+ organizations across 120 countries.**

Small studios, large real estate groups, construction companies, consultants of the built world: **Rayon’s adopters span across the** _**entire**_ **industry.**

It’s never too early or too late to make the switch. Rayon works today as well in new agencies, kickstarting their practice (Identité, Adrien Dupuy, etc), all the way to established businesses looking to level up their existing workflows (Wojo, Halkin, the Engine, etc).

*   **Kyka's architects** works **3x faster** on their drawing sets by switching all their workflows onto Rayon.
    
*   **CityHub** saves **€10k/month** by using Rayon for feasibility studies.
    
*   **Wojo** has **moved their entire sales force and facility management** to Rayon.
    

Among many others, here are a few of the other companies that recently made the switch...

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/others/switching-to-rayon#how-does-switching-work)

How does switching work?

There are **multiple ways to switch to Rayon**, and you can transition your company at your own pace. You can **get started in minutes** by following the steps below, or **get in touch** with our team so we can help with your migration…

**1) Start simple: create an account**

*   Rayon is simpler to access than legacy software; all you need is a browser.
    
*   To get started, you can [create an account right here](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/signup)
    .
    
*   Everything about Rayon signup steps [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/signing-up)
    .
    

**Tip** — We recommend you install our native app, to access Rayon faster. [Download page here](https://www.rayon.design/download)
.

**2) Work with the data you already have: DWG / CTB / PDF, etc**

*   **Rayon allows you to work with the files you already have** (DWG, PDFs, Images).
    
*   **DWG** can be read entirely. Rayon transposes their entire layer structure, blocks, hatch files etc. Import is lossless, making you feel like you started within a CAD software you already know.
    
*   **CTBs** can be entirely replicated easily in Rayon, by using Rayon's styles. More on this [topic right here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)
    .
    

**Tip** — We recommend you watch [our import tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WIjh2zLJJpk)
, to get familiarized with our DWG support.

**3) Draft like you know how**

*   **Drawing habits from legacy CAD softwares translate in Rayon, to make you feel at home:** Rayon works with a command line, tools can be called using shortcuts, drawing are organized with layers, etc.
    
*   Everything about Rayon's design experience [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design)
    .
    

**Tip** — To get started with Rayon's design experience, [we recommend you watch this short demo](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sCD0FcOelqY)
.

**4) Set up your libraries and templates**

*   In Rayon, blocks and styles can be turned into libraries to share with your colleagues.
    
*   Drawings can be turned into templates, to get your entire team on the same graphic standards.
    
*   Everything about libraries and templates [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing/publishing-a-library)
    .
    

**Tip** — To get started with libraries and templates, we recommend [you to watch this demo](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Bnt04SK4C5Q&list=PL2mYb69TvSpw4sO2nADaUQpYXbzMe_z59&index=17)
.

**5) Gather your team**

*   Rayon is a **multiplayer software**.
    
*   It is the first software for architects that finally brings live co-editing to design teams.
    
*   Additionally, Rayon allows you to comment/annotate your work, to make sure your team stays in sync.
    
*   Finally, Rayon provides a team-wide file system, enabling you to organize and share models and resources across your entire organization.
    
*   Everything about setting up your organization [can be found here](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing/organizations)
    , while everything about Rayon's collaboration layer [can be found at this link](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayons-basics/sharing-commenting-annotating)
    .
    

**Tip** — To set up your team in Rayon in a few minutes, we recommend [you to watch this short tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=b5tDNGqXWfQ)
.

**Ready switch?** Then simply signup today, book a demo with our team, or check our training portal!

[](https://www.rayon.design/app/auth/signup)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_ca173227e9)

A new version of Rayon is here, and we have a lot of new things for you…

Here is a sneak peek at new things ✨

*   The Walls
    
*   The Tables
    

Here is a sneak peek at things that got better 💪

*   The Styles
    

For a more in-depth look at Rayon’s features, 👉 [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_b7aae9ae5f)

Some Things are New ✨


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_fd300bca2a)

Walls ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F626313243%2F2aa0f5915d30fe26d404432a%2Fwall-create.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4649c584&sv=2)

Drawing a plan is mostly about **laying down walls and partitions.**

Rayon now allows you to draw such walls, snap windows and doors in them, and mark room surfaces using Zones. 👉 More about this new feature [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/elements-walls-zones-openings-etc)
 🔗

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_11f04817a7)

Tables ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F626313997%2F8ae3745997055e0c0a4b121b%2Ftables.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c0a5deb&sv=2)

People like to **list and count objects in floor plans.**

That's why we built the tables: in just a few clicks, you can now give properties to objects, list them and keep quantities in check. 👉 More about this new feature in our Documentation! 🔗

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_bad6a3691e)

Some Things got Better 💪


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1#h_2d62b02d60)

Styles 💪

*   Styles have been improved!
    
*   We now have a revamped placing of active styles and selected styles; Simply, a new (and easier) way to work with styles in Rayon

# March 2023 Changelog | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMBzpClywmaloH1aut0Oj%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c5a18f2-f572-428e-bb06-52ee67de9e10&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f06d1a0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/march-2023-changelog#weve-made-some-improvements-to-selected-features-to-make-your-rayon-experience-seamless)

We've made some improvements to selected features to make your Rayon experience seamless!

Here is what got better 💪

*   Blocks: scaling text
    
*   Style: texture offset and rotation by individual zone
    
*   Tables: 'group by' option
    

For a more in-depth look at Rayon's features, 👉 [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/march-2023-changelog#h_32cfab8531)

Features that got better 💪


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/march-2023-changelog#h_21f7f0d926)

Blocks: scaling text 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F684819076%2Fad98bbe45ee755832ed9a6dc%2Fezgif.com-gif-maker%2B%25288%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e6f697c&sv=2)

Text embedded within a block does now scale seamlessly! 👉 More about Blocks [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/march-2023-changelog#h_b32143cb14)

Style: texture offset and rotation by individual zone 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F684817551%2F66e559adc7161ab10058dae6%2Fezgif.com-gif-maker%2B%25287%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ffadb09&sv=2)

From now on, zones with the same texture style can be controlled independently to set their offset and rotation! 👉 More about Styles [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/march-2023-changelog#h_1dfa727110)

Tables: 'group by' option 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F684816358%2F111e3e59322742bb289866d9%2Fezgif.com-gif-maker%2B%25286%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c341e542&sv=2)

Tables are meant to list and count elements on a floor plan. Now, you can also group these elements! 👉 More about Tables in our Documentation!

* * *

# April 2023 Changelog | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMBzpClywmaloH1aut0Oj%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c5a18f2-f572-428e-bb06-52ee67de9e10&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f06d1a0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#we-are-constantly-working-on-improving-and-revamping-rayons-features-for-our-users)

We are constantly working on improving and revamping Rayon's features for our users!

Here are new features that just got better💪

*   New pages system
    
*   Improved wall drawing experience
    
*   New dashed lines styles
    

For a more in-depth look at Rayon's features, 👉 [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#h_8e9374accb)

Features that got better 💪


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#h_3369ac7cdb)

New pages system 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F709486505%2F7899570673aea3ce34918ac7%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%252843%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dc7b14d3&sv=2)

You can now "Nest" items onto a page! This will enable you to scale the page's content before exporting it to a PDF. 👉 More about Pages in our Documentation!

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#h_64ae6b9c71)

Improved wall drawing experience 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F707725814%2Fc25a214d4a6c17ac0ab59e25%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%252838%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a7ad554&sv=2)

You can now shift the wall center line left or right for a more precise drawing experience! 👉 More about Walls [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/elements-walls-zones-openings-etc)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#h_7039182f95)

New dashed lines styles 💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F707732292%2F3cd9c10b1e891feb2dd046fb%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%252839%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7466fa30&sv=2)

We have revamped the dash line families to offer you a greater variety! 👉 More about Line Styles [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)

* * *

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/april-2023-changelog#h_ba9ac3c1c9)

Any questions? ☝️


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Rayon V1 RC | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMBzpClywmaloH1aut0Oj%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c5a18f2-f572-428e-bb06-52ee67de9e10&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f06d1a0&sv=2)

Nov. 15th '22

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_072000814c)

You asked, we listened! 🎉


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_25228b0941)

A new version of Rayon is here, and we have a lot of new things for you…

Here is a sneak peek at **new things** ✨

*   The Quick Action Bar
    
*   The Dimension Tool
    
*   The Right-Click
    
*   The Active Bar
    

Here is a sneak peek at **things that got better** 💪

*   The Styles
    
*   The Layers
    
*   The DWG/DXF Import
    

For a more in-depth look at Rayon’s features, 👉 [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_b80cd1d516)

Some Things are New ✨


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_8c44160eda)

Quick Actions ✨

We know that editing things should be fast. That’s why we just created the **quick action bar!** This bar **shows up each time you select something** and gives you access to fast, off-the-shelf actions (alignment, rotation, flipping, deleting, hiding, locking).

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_a24457b659)

Dimensions ✨

Rayon now allows you to draw dimensions. The dimensions command can be found in the toolbar and enables users to **quickly mark distances on their plans.**

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_5a49cb93e7)

Right Click ✨

Having a right click is a must-have, and it is now something you have in Rayon. Right-clicking on the canvas will give you **a quick way to access a whole lot of options** (clipboards, transform, Help… To get to the documentation, and many other things)!

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_f7db51cd81)

Some Things Got Better 💪


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_6b161785d7)

Styles 💪

Styles have been improved. It is now much **easier to edit, manage, and swap styles** in your drawing.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_3ab78caf83)

Layers 💪

Layers have been revamped to make sure it gets easier to work with them. **Shuffling items, editing groups, and blocks, but also simply visualizing selected elements** in the layer panel, got a whole lot simpler.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_85253cbc5f)

DWG/DXF Import 💪

Importing CAD files can be a pain. We made things much simpler; when importing a DWG or DXF file to your workspace, we offer you **a few simple steps to make sure the model units and size are just fine.**

* * *

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/rayon-v1-rc#h_07a2db82ff)

Any questions? ☝️


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\-> Feel free to email us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.rayon.design/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 🙌

→ For a more in-depth look at Rayon’s features, [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)
 🔗

# February 2023 Changelog | Rayon Docs 

![Page cover](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112124689-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FngVHKyaUSSJPTFck3wkz%252Fuploads%252FMBzpClywmaloH1aut0Oj%252Fdocumentation-header-desktop.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c5a18f2-f572-428e-bb06-52ee67de9e10&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f06d1a0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#we-are-happy-to-share-the-progress-and-features-added-in-rayon-to-make-drawing-faster-and-easier-for)

We are happy to share the progress and features added in Rayon to make drawing faster and easier for you!

Here are the new things that were added this month✨

*   Patterns
    
*   Annotations
    
*   Boolean operations
    
*   Zone divider
    
*   Arc
    
*   Match properties
    

And here is what got better 💪

*   Offsetting door & window openings
    
*   PDF import
    

For a more in-depth look at Rayon's features, 👉 [check out the Documentation](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/rayon-documentation)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_856d745d06)

Some things are new ✨


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_ac15cd7bb0)

Patterns ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F673958355%2Fd201354f4ad69d687566c8a3%2Fezgif.com-optimize.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7801dfc&sv=2)

Floor plans commonly include hatches and textures for informative reasons (indicating the material) and aesthetic reasons (preparing a drawing for presentation). From now on, **choose a pattern and edit it with advanced options** - all on the Rayon canvas.

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_a9289df422)

Annotations ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675308713%2F576693fd8a16457ceab9c32f%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25281%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e121bca0&sv=2)

Adding information to your floor plan can now be done faster using **customized annotations:** straight or curved, one or double-sided Arrows, pins, and more!

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_1b0c0d40bf)

Boolean operations ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675311140%2F64ad51cc8749f6a82774379f%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25282%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e3ef592&sv=2)

Draw **complex shapes** with the new boolean operation feature enabling you to:

*   Subtract
    
*   Union
    
*   Intersect
    
*   Exclude
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_d5ed0ae669)

Zone divider ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675313371%2Fa94381179c9d6073efe60b4b%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25283%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a08ceed9&sv=2)

Often, open space areas have sub-divisions according to their use case. That's why we've added a Zone Divider, allowing you to **add a zone freely, with no wall partition**. 👉 More about the wall and zone features [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/elements-walls-zones-openings-etc)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_0c4abcaaaa)

Arc ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675316737%2F3fdeb2cb5e12a7c077e14fba%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25284%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98f72e96&sv=2)

The editing tools now include an Arc! You can implement it in 2 ways:

*   By using the arc tool to draw an arc.
    
*   By drawing a polyline and implementing an arc as a part of it: either click on the `**Arc (AC)**` or on the `**Line (L)**` to go between a straight or arched line!
    

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_d08d0e4859)

Match properties ✨

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F682632684%2Fcf80941ef6fd53c01d8392a9%2FMatchprop.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71167526&sv=2)

You can now use the `**eyedropper**` button to match the style properties of elements on the canvas! 👉 More about the style properties [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/design/styles)

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_3b3347190f)

And some are better 💪


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_d4b2155bce)

Offsetting door & window openings💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675319492%2F17a7a3e0f1fea8e84208ad26%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25285%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ac34630&sv=2)

When adding an opening block such as a door or a window, hover over it to detect the light blue dashed line: then **drag it to determine the offsetting** of the component! 👉 More about opening and furniture blocks [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/publishing-and-sharing)

### 

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_1188b12203)

PDF import💪

![](https://docs.rayon.design/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F675946029%2F40539380e5eeb1effa9ef7f3%2Fezgif.com-optimize%2B%25286%2529.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2da34b2&sv=2)

When importing a PDF file, Rayon will ask you to **set an estimated distance for reference**. This will help scale and **convert the PDF file into a Rayon model**. 👉 More about importing, exporting, and sharing [in our Documentation!](https://docs.rayon.design/documentation/team-management-and-billing)

* * *

[](https://docs.rayon.design/other-resources/product-updates/february-2023-changelog#h_0df20bdc5e)

Any questions? ☝️


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 🙌

# Email Protection | Cloudflare

Please enable cookies.

Email Protection
================

You are unable to access this email address docs.rayon.design
-------------------------------------------------------------

The website from which you got to this page is protected by Cloudflare. Email addresses on that page have been hidden in order to keep them from being accessed by malicious bots. **You must enable Javascript in your browser in order to decode the e-mail address**.

If you have a website and are interested in protecting it in a similar way, you can [sign up for Cloudflare](https://www.cloudflare.com/sign-up?utm_source=email_protection)
.

*   [How does Cloudflare protect email addresses on website from spammers?](https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/tools/scrape-shield/email-address-obfuscation/)
    
*   [Can I sign up for Cloudflare?](https://developers.cloudflare.com/fundamentals/setup/account/create-account/)
